    function (e, t, r) {
        var o = r(28),
            f = r(23),
            n = r(50),
            a = r(29);

        function i(e) {
            this.options = $.extend({}, {
                container: "#table_wrapper",
                name: "",
                type: "",
                time: 0,
                fields: "f1,f2,f3,f4,f5,f12,f13,f14,f108,f152,f161,f249,f250,f330,f334,f339,f340,f341,f342,f343,f344,f345,f346,f347",
                px: "f161",
                pageIndex: 1,
                pageSize: 20,
                po: 0,
                ut: "bd1d9ddb04089700cf9c27f6f7426281",
                orderBy: "xqj",
                sort: "asc",
                cp: "c"
            }, e), this.page = new a, this.cacheName = this.options.name + (this.options.type + "").substring(2), this.heads = n.txbj, this.initDom()
        }
        i.prototype.initDom = function () {
            $(".tx_header").length && $(".tx_header").remove();
            var e = '<div class="tx_header"><div><div class="left">' + this.options.name + '认购期权</div><div class="center"><select class="tx_dete" id="tx_dete"></select></div><div class="right">' + this.options.name + "认沽期权</div></div></div>";
            $(this.options.container).prepend(e), this.$table = $(this.options.container).find("#table_wrapper-table"), this.$table.addClass("tx_table"), this.loadDate(), this.event()
        }, i.prototype.pageClick = function () {
            var e = this;
            e.page.onPage = function (t) {
                e.options.pageIndex = t, t > e.options.sumPage && (e.options.pageIndex = e.options.sumPage), e.update()
            }
        }, i.prototype.loadDate = function () {
            var e = this,
                t = o.getEnvPath("tsApi") + "api/qt/stock/get";
            $.ajax({
                url: t,
                method: "GET",
                data: {
                    mspt: 1,
                    secid: this.options.type,
                    ut: this.options.ut
                },
                dataType: "jsonp",
                jsonp: "cb",
                success: function (t) {
                    if (t && t.data && t.data.optionExpireInfo) {
                        for (var r = t.data.optionExpireInfo || [], o = "", f = 0, n = 0; n < r.length; n++) {
                            var a = r[n].date + "",
                                i = a.substring(0, 6),
                                s = a.substring(0, 4) + "年" + parseInt(a.substring(4, 6)) + "月(" + r[n].days + "天)",
                                l = "";
                            localStorage.getItem(e.cacheName) === i && (l = "selected", e.options.time = i), o += '<option value="' + i + '" ' + l + ">" + s + "</option>", 0 === n && (f = i)
                        }
                        $("#tx_dete").html(o), e.options.time || (e.options.time = f)
                    }
                    e.update()
                }, error: function (t) {
                    console && console.log(t), e.update()
                }
            })
        }, i.prototype.createThead = function () {
            for (var e = this.heads.head, t = [], r = 0; r < e.length; r++) {
                var o = e[r];
                if (o) {
                    var f = o.order ? "sorting" : "",
                        n = "";
                    this.options.px === o.key && (n = 0 === this.options.po ? "sorting_asc" : "sorting_desc"), o.tips ? t.push('<th class="' + f + " " + n + '"  data-key="' + o.key + '"><span title="' + o.tips + '"><span>' + o.title + '</span><b class="icon_yiwen"></b></span><b class="icon"></b></th>') : t.push('<th class="' + f + " " + n + '"  data-key="' + o.key + '"><span>' + o.title + '</span><b class="icon"></b></th>')
                }
            }
            this.$table.find("thead").html(t.join(""))
        }, i.prototype.update = function () {
            var e = this;
            e.createThead(), e.gehqtData((function (t) {
                if (t && t.data && t.data.diff) {
                    var r = t.data.total,
                        o = Math.ceil(r / e.options.pageSize);
                    e.options.sumPage = o, o > 1 ? (e.page.setOps({
                        index: e.options.pageIndex,
                        sumPage: e.options.sumPage
                    }), e.pageClick(), $(".dataTables_paginate").show()) : $(".dataTables_paginate").hide(), e.loadTable(t.data.diff)
                } else e.errorLoad()
            }))
        }, i.prototype.errorLoad = function () {
            this.$table.find("tbody").html(""), $(".dataTables_paginate").hide()
        }, i.prototype.gehqtData = function (e) {
            var t = this,
                r = o.getEnvPath("tsApi") + "api/qt/slist/get",
                f = {
                    secid: this.options.type,
                    exti: this.options.time,
                    spt: 9,
                    fltt: 2,
                    invt: 2,
                    np: 1,
                    ut: this.options.ut,
                    fields: this.options.fields,
                    fid: this.options.px,
                    pn: this.options.pageIndex,
                    pz: this.options.pageSize,
                    po: this.options.po
                };
            $.ajax({
                url: r,
                method: "GET",
                data: f,
                dataType: "jsonp",
                jsonp: "cb",
                success: function (t) {
                    e && e(t)
                }, error: function (e) {
                    t.errorLoad(), console && console.log(e)
                }
            })
        }, i.prototype.loadTable = function (e) {
            for (var t = "", r = 0; r < e.length; r++) {
                var o = e[r],
                    n = {
                        gouName: o.f14,
                        gouCode: o.f12,
                        gouMarket: o.f13,
                        gouZxj: f.formatNumberFlag(o.f2, o.f1),
                        gouZdf: f.formatNumberIndexZdf(o.f3, o.f152),
                        gouZde: f.formatNumberFlag(o.f4, o.f1),
                        gouCcl: o.f108,
                        gouCjl: o.f5,
                        gouYxbd: f.toPercent(o.f249, 2),
                        gouZYjl: f.toPercent(o.f250, 2),
                        Xqj: f.formatNumberFlag(o.f161, o.f330),
                        guName: o.f340,
                        guCode: o.f339,
                        guMarket: o.f13,
                        guZxj: f.formatNumberFlag(o.f341, o.f1),
                        guZdf: f.formatNumberIndexZdf(o.f343, o.f152),
                        guZde: f.formatNumberFlag(o.f342, o.f1),
                        guCcl: f.formatNumberFlag(o.f345),
                        guCjl: f.formatNumber(o.f344),
                        guYxbd: f.toPercent(o.f346, 2),
                        guZYjl: f.toPercent(o.f347, 2)
                    },
                    a = f.getColor(o.f161, o.f334, ["bgLightGreen", "bgLightRed"]),
                    i = f.getColor(o.f161, o.f334, ["bgLightRed", "bgLightGreen"]),
                    s = f.getColor(o.f4),
                    l = f.getColor(o.f342);
                t += '<tr><td class="' + a + '"><a href="' + f.quoteLink(n.gouCode, n.gouMarket) + '" target="_blank">' + n.gouName + '</a></td><td class="' + a + '"><span class="' + s + '">' + n.gouZxj + '</span></td><td class="' + a + '"><span class="' + s + '">' + n.gouZdf + '</span></td><td class="' + a + '"><span class="' + s + '">' + n.gouZde + '</span></td><td class="' + a + '"><span >' + n.gouCcl + '</span></td><td class="' + a + '"><span >' + n.gouCjl + '</span></td><td class="' + a + '"><span >' + n.gouYxbd + '</span></td><td class="' + a + '"><span >' + n.gouZYjl + '</span></td><td class="xq_orange"><span >' + n.Xqj + '</span></td><td class="' + i + '"><a href="' + f.quoteLink(n.guCode, n.guMarket) + '" target="_blank">' + n.guName + '</a></td><td class="' + i + '"><span class="' + l + '">' + n.guZxj + '</span></td><td class="' + i + '"><span class="' + l + '">' + n.guZdf + '</span></td><td class="' + i + '"><span class="' + l + '">' + n.guZde + '</span></td><td class="' + i + '"><span >' + n.guCcl + '</span></td><td class="' + i + '"><span >' + n.guCjl + '</span></td><td class="' + i + '"><span >' + n.guYxbd + '</span></td><td class="' + i + '"><span >' + n.guZYjl + "</span></td></tr>"
            }
            this.$table.find("tbody").html(t), localStorage.setItem(this.cacheName, this.options.time)
        }, i.prototype.event = function () {
            var e = this;
            $("#tx_dete").change((function () {
                e.options.time = $(this).val(), e.options.pageIndex = 1, e.update()
            })), e.$table.find("thead").off(), e.$table.find("thead").on("click", "th.sorting", (function (t) {
                t.stopPropagation(), t.preventDefault();

                } catch (e) {} - 1 === location.hash.indexOf("_txbj") && ($("#table_wrapper-table").removeClass("tx_table"), $(".tx_header").remove())

                    cp: this.options.cp,
                    blockName: "txdate"
                };
            a(t, this.url, (function (t) {
                if (t && t.date && t.date.length) {
                    for (var r = t.date || [], o = "", f = 0, n = 0; n < r.length; n++) {
                        var a = r[n].date + "",
                            i = a.substring(0, 4) + "年" + parseInt(a.substring(4, 6)) + "月(" + r[n].remainDay + "天)",
                            s = "";
                        localStorage.getItem(e.cacheName) === a && (s = "selected", e.options.time = a), o += '<option value="' + a + '" ' + s + ">" + i + "</option>", 0 === n && (f = a)
                    }
                    $("#tx_dete").html(o), e.options.time || (e.options.time = f)
                }
                e.update()
            }))
        }, s.prototype.createThead = function () {
            for (var e = this.heads.head, t = [], r = 0; r < e.length; r++) {
                var o = e[r],
                    f = o.order ? "sorting" : "",
                    n = "";
                this.options.orderBy === o.key && this.options.cp === o.type && (n = "asc" === this.options.sort ? "sorting_asc" : "sorting_desc"), o.tips ? t.push('<th class="' + f + " " + n + '"  data-key="' + o.key + "|" + o.type + '"><span title="' + o.tips + '"><span>' + o.title + '</span><b class="icon_yiwen"></b></span><b class="icon"></b></th>') : t.push('<th class="' + f + " " + n + '"  data-key="' + o.key + "|" + o.type + '"><span>' + o.title + '</span><b class="icon"></b></th>')
            }
            this.$table.find("thead").html(t.join(""))
        }, s.prototype.update = function () {
            var e = this;
            e.createThead(), e.gehqtData((function (t) {
                if (t && t.list && t.list.length) {
                    var r = t.total,
                        o = Math.ceil(r / e.options.pageSize);
                    e.options.sumPage = o, o > 1 ? (e.page.setOps({
                        index: e.options.pageIndex,
                        sumPage: e.options.sumPage
                    }), e.pageClick(), $(".dataTables_paginate").show()) : $(".dataTables_paginate").hide(), e.loadTable(t.list)
                } else e.errorLoad()
            }))
        }, s.prototype.errorLoad = function () {
            this.$table.find("tbody").html(""), $(".dataTables_paginate").hide()
        }, s.prototype.gehqtData = function (e) {
            var t = {
                orderBy: this.options.orderBy,
                sort: this.options.sort,
                pageSize: this.options.pageSize,
                pageIndex: this.options.pageIndex - 1,
                cp: this.options.cp,
                date: this.options.time,
                blockName: "txdata"
            };
            a(t, this.url, (function (t) {
                e && e(t)
            }))
        }, s.prototype.loadTable = function (e) {
            for (var t = "", r = 0; r < e.length; r++) {
                var o = e[r].callQt,
                    n = e[r].putQt,
                    a = {
                        gouName: o.name,
                        gouCode: o.sc,
                        gouMarket: o.dm,
                        gouZxj: f.formatNumberFlag(o.p, o.zsjd),
                        gouZdf: f.formatNumberIndexZdf(o.zdf, 2),
                        gouZde: f.formatNumberFlag(o.zde, o.zsjd),
                        gouCcl: f.formatNumber(o.ccl),
                        gouCjl: f.formatNumber(o.vol),
                        gouYxbd: f.toPercent(o.yhbdl, 2),
                        gouZYjl: f.toPercent(o.zyjl, 2),
                        Xqj: f.formatNumberFlag(o.xqj, 0),
                        guName: n.name,
                        guCode: n.sc,
                        guMarket: n.dm,
                        guZxj: f.formatNumberFlag(n.p, n.zsjd),
                        guZdf: f.formatNumberIndexZdf(n.zdf, 2),
                        guZde: f.formatNumberFlag(n.zde, n.zsjd),
                        guCcl: f.formatNumberFlag(n.ccl),
                        guCjl: f.formatNumber(n.vol),
                        guYxbd: f.toPercent(n.yhbdl, 2),
                        guZYjl: f.toPercent(n.zyjl, 2)
                    },
                    i = f.getColor(o.bddqj, o.xqj, ["bgLightRed", "bgLightGreen"]),
                    s = f.getColor(n.bddqj, o.xqj, ["bgLightRed", "bgLightGreen"]),
                    l = f.getColor(o.zde),
                    u = f.getColor(n.zde);
                t += '<tr><td class="' + i + '"><a href="' + f.quoteLink(a.gouMarket, a.gouCode) + '" target="_blank">' + a.gouName + '</a></td><td class="' + i + '"><span class="' + l + '">' + a.gouZxj + '</span></td><td class="' + i + '"><span class="' + l + '">' + a.gouZdf + '</span></td><td class="' + i + '"><span class="' + l + '">' + a.gouZde + '</span></td><td class="' + i + '"><span >' + a.gouCcl + '</span></td><td class="' + i + '"><span >' + a.gouCjl + '</span></td><td class="' + i + '"><span >' + a.gouYxbd + '</span></td><td class="' + i + '"><span >' + a.gouZYjl + '</span></td><td class="xq_orange"><span >' + a.Xqj + '</span></td><td class="' + s + '"><a href="' + f.quoteLink(a.guMarket, a.guCode) + '" target="_blank">' + a.guName + '</a></td><td class="' + s + '"><span class="' + u + '">' + a.guZxj + '</span></td><td class="' + s + '"><span class="' + u + '">' + a.guZdf + '</span></td><td class="' + s + '"><span class="' + u + '">' + a.guZde + '</span></td><td class="' + s + '"><span >' + a.guCcl + '</span></td><td class="' + s + '"><span >' + a.guCjl + '</span></td><td class="' + s + '"><span >' + a.guYxbd + '</span></td><td class="' + s + '"><span >' + a.guZYjl + "</span></td></tr>"
            }
            this.$table.find("tbody").html(t), localStorage.setItem(this.cacheName, this.options.time)
        }, s.prototype.event = function () {
            var e = this;
            $("#tx_dete").change((function () {
                e.options.time = $(this).val(), e.options.pageIndex = 1, e.update()
            })), e.$table.find("thead").off(), e.$table.find("thead").on("click", "th.sorting", (function (t) {
                t.stopPropagation(), t.preventDefault();
                var r = $(this).data("key");
                r && (e.options.orderBy + "|" + e.options.cp === r ? e.options.sort = "asc" === e.options.sort ? "desc" : "asc" : (r = r.split("|"), e.options.orderBy = r[0], e.options.cp = r[1]), e.update())
            })), $(window).hashchange((function (e) {
                try {
                    clearInterval(window.cd)
                } catch (e) {} - 1 === location.hash.indexOf("_txbj") && ($("#table_wrapper-table").removeClass("tx_table"), $(".tx_header").hide())
            }))
        }, e.exports = s
    }
]);
